Wuhan University Petition Delegation Goes to Peiping 72

Second Middle School Suggests that all Middle Schools Continue to Go to Peiping

Hankou Correspondence - More than 150 people from the National Wuhan University petition delegation, divided into four teams and sixteen groups, took the China Merchants Bureau's Jiangjing Wheel to Peiping on the evening of the 4th. The highest command of the organization was the Executive Committee, with one chief commander and one deputy commander. Each team had a team leader, and each group had a group leader. On the afternoon of that day, the entire petition delegation, led by Executive Director Wang Chuanzeng, Commander Yin Dekun, Deputy Commander Yan Guangzhi, Team Leader Chen Guangzhu, and Group Leader Cai Renxi, took an oath and set off. President Wang Shijie personally wrote a hand-written note stipulating eight points to be observed in terms of discipline and thirteen measures for punishing violations of discipline, which were mimeographed and distributed to all members to be strictly observed. It is heard that the main points of the petition are divided into six items: (1) Deny the establishment of the Jinzhou Neutral Zone; (2) Request the government to withdraw from the League of Nations; (3) Sever diplomatic relations with Japan and implement the recovery of lost territory by force; (4) Complete peaceful unification; (5) Allow General Zhang Fakui to send troops north immediately; (6) Provide practical assistance to General Ma Zhanshan and issue a declaration urging the government to abandon its policy of non-resistance and no longer rely on the League of Nations, but to fight the Japanese imperialists with blood and heads. They vowed not to return to school if they did not receive a satisfactory response. The students who remained at school decided to set aside the week from the 4th to the 10th as National Crisis Week, suspend classes, intensify military training, and hold lectures on the Sino-Japanese incident to study the anti-Japanese policy. Other schools have not yet organized petition delegations to Peiping. However, the Provincial Second Middle School decided on the 4th to suggest to the Wuhan Academic Anti-Japanese General Association that they organize petition delegations from various middle schools to Peiping to request a declaration of war against Japan (December 4).

Ironclad Proof that the Japanese Military and Civilians Unanimously Plot Against Us 73

The Wokou's Plot to Seize Our Northeast is Entirely Unanimous Between Military and Civilians

It is often said that years of aggressive behavior are all the actions of the tyrannical military factions of their country, and that their people are not like this. Alas, this is a fallacious theory that misleads the country! Now, we have found a copy of the recent resolutions of the "Japanese Residents in Manchuria Emergency Support Association," the content of which is outrageous and infuriating. Isn't this the general mentality of their people? Can it still be said that their people are not the echo of the Tanaka policy? We have translated the various items in the document to alert the people of the country and to prove that there is no meaning in the unanimity of the violent Japanese military and civilians. Now that the Japanese are holding their so-called "All China Residents' General Assembly" in Shanghai, what they resolve should exceed what is contained in this document. When the people of the country read this, they should be able to see Sima Zhao's intentions! The original text is as follows:

Resolutions of the Japanese Residents in Manchuria Emergency Support Association

I. Regarding Political, Military, and Diplomatic Matters

(1) Regarding the Sino-Japanese incident, absolutely reject the intervention of the League of Nations and third countries. When necessary, we will not hesitate to withdraw from the League of Nations.

(2) Regarding the four northeastern provinces, the Zhang Xueliang faction is a revival of the old regime and will absolutely not be recognized.

(3) We expect the rapid realization of an independent state in the four northeastern provinces.

(4) When resolving the situation, all matters concerning the four northeastern provinces should be negotiated with the aforementioned independent state.

(5) To protect Japanese rights and interests in the four northeastern provinces and the lives and property of the two million Japanese residents, we hope that imperial troops will be dispatched to necessary locations.

(6) The Chinese challenges of anti-Japanese humiliation and anti-Japanese goods should be thoroughly abolished and punished.

(7) When the central regime of the four northeastern provinces establishes a fixed independent country, it should guide and supervise its political administration to ensure the practical resolution of our required pending cases.

II. Regarding Transportation and Communication Matters

(1) The Chinese state-owned railways and ports in the four northeastern provinces should be managed by Japan at least until the situation is resolved.

(2) Various railways belonging to our vested rights should be laid immediately.

(3) Railways that violate transportation treaties and infringe on our rights and interests should be removed.

III. Regarding Financial, Fiscal, and Tariff Matters

(1) The collection of tariffs and taxes outside of treaties in the four northeastern provinces should be absolutely abolished.

(2) Financial institutions in the four northeastern provinces should be quickly established to promote currency integration.

IV. Regarding Commercial, Industrial, Agricultural, Forestry, and Mining Matters

(1) The vested rights of Japanese nationals in the forests, mines, agriculture, and commerce and industry of the four northeastern provinces, whether they are joint ventures or not, should be immediately restored and realized.

(2) The obstacles to Sino-Japanese two-way and general commercial relations in the four northeastern provinces caused by the situation should be quickly rectified to promote their smooth development.

(3) Civil and criminal lawsuits and disputes between Chinese and Japanese parties in the four northeastern provinces should be handled by imperial officials until the situation is resolved.

Hu Hanmin Hastily Returns to Guangdong 74

After Paying Respects to the Late Gu Yingfen, He Attended One Meeting

He and Mr. Wu Chaoshu Departed for Hong Kong Again That Afternoon

Guangzhou Correspondence: After the breakdown of the Fourth Plenary Session of the Guangdong Provincial Party Congress, Mr. Hu Zhantang, who had been residing in Shanghai after the departure of Sun Ke and the Wang Jingwei faction's representatives to Hong Kong, went south with Wu Chaoshu and others, intending to mediate. When Hu and his party arrived in Hong Kong, Sun Ke, Chen Youren, Li Wenfan, and others had also arrived in Hong Kong from Macau and held secret talks with Mr. Hu. Hu originally intended to mediate between the two sides in Hong Kong, but because six or seven representatives from Guangdong personally went to Hong Kong to welcome Mr. Hu to the province, Hu believed that it was his close friend Gu Xiangqin's burial on the 29th, which the National Government adorned with state funeral rites, and that it was proper for him to personally attend the funeral, to fulfill the friendship of life and death. Therefore, Hu took the Jinshan steamer from Hong Kong on the evening of the 28th and arrived in the province at 6:30 AM on the 29th. The provincial authorities, having heard the news beforehand, dispatched a large number of military police to guard the wharf and the roads. Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, Bai Chongxi, Lin Yunhai, heads of various institutions, representatives of the Fourth Plenary Session, and others, about several hundred in number, waited in front of the wharf. Automobiles with flags high above, reading "Welcome Mr. Hu Hanmin back to Guangdong to preside over major plans," caused heavy traffic and great excitement. After the ship docked, Hu, accompanied by his daughter, Mulan, and Wu Chaoshu, disembarked. Those who followed included Secretary Wang Yangchong and Li Xiangen. Mr. Hu had been away from Guangdong for more than ten years, and this time, returning to his hometown, many old friends welcomed him. On that day, Mr. Hu wore a long cotton gown and a black mandarin jacket, appearing more gaunt than before, but still with a dashing manner. When he walked out of the wharf, due to the crowd, only Chen Jitang and a few others were able to shake hands with Hu; the rest were unable to get close. Chen Jitang then helped Mr. Hu into a car and drove straight to Gu Yingfen's ancestral hall on Cangbian Street to pay respects. Hu was very saddened when he paid respects to Gu, crying bitterly and fainting twice. Fortunately, his daughter Mulan and Gu's relative, Wu Zhimei, were by his side to support him for a long time before leading him upstairs to rest. Hu originally arranged to talk with the welcomers at the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall at noon, but because he was extremely sad at this time and his spirit was weary, he broke his appointment. The welcomers and representatives of various groups waited until the afternoon before dispersing. The authorities, considering that Hu was not feeling well and had chosen Yulu in Ershatou, Dongshan, as Hu's residence, Hu went to Yulu at 1:00 PM. Soon after, leaders of the party, military, and government arrived one after another. In addition to Hu and Wu Chaoshu, those who attended included Chen Jitang, Li Zongren, Huang Xuchu, Xiang Hanping, Deng Zheru, Xiao Focheng, Ma Chaojun, Lin Yun, Chen Ce, Li Yangjing, Feng Zhuwan, Chen Rong, Lin Yizhong, Yu Hanmou, Zhang Huichang, and others. A meeting was held to discuss the current situation, and various issues regarding the resolution of the situation were discussed. The details of the meeting were kept secret. According to outside reports, the resolutions of the Shanghai peace conference still need to be revised. The meeting lasted until about 3:00 PM. After the meeting, those around Hu, seeing that Hu was tired from the day's engagements and that his blood pressure had gradually increased due to excessive crying for Gu, advised Hu to go to Hong Kong for medical treatment. Therefore, Hu hurriedly took the Jinshan night boat to Hong Kong at 4:00 PM on the 29th, arriving in Hong Kong at 11:50 PM that evening. It is said that Hu may return to Guangdong to discuss major plans after resting in Hong Kong for a day or two. Another view is that whether Hu will visit Guangdong again is still questionable. Nanhui 77

Nanhui Representatives Come to the Provincial Capital to Petition on the Boundary Issue: Twenty-two representatives from Nanhui, including Chen Moquan, came to the provincial capital yesterday to petition on the issue of the demarcation of the boundary between Nanhui and Fengxian. It is reported that this issue arose because Fengxian wanted to划take the old Taiping Township and part of the old Duxing Township of Nanhui under its jurisdiction. Nanhui had convened a boundary committee meeting of local agencies and groups by the county government. The result of the discussion was that Fengxian's claim was groundless. Because the change in the administrative region of the county is compiled and prepared in accordance with the "Outline of the Administrative District or Organization of the County" promulgated by the Ministry of Internal Affairs, even if there are circumstances stipulated in Article 7 of the "Provincial, Municipal, and County Surveying Boundaries," the change in organization must be based on significant administrative inconveniences. The jurisdiction of the old Taiping Township and other areas under Nanhui does not have this kind of shortcoming for Fengxian. Therefore, various agencies and groups such as the County Chamber of Commerce and the Fund Property Office held a boundary protection movement conference in Biyutang on the 29th. Hundreds of representatives from all walks of life and residents of Taiping Township unanimously opposed being劃taken into Fengxian's jurisdiction, and elected the Fund Property Office Chen Moquan, County Chamber of Commerce Pan Ziping, County Education Association Zhao Xinmei, County Party Department Zhu Jiming, Education Bureau Shi Shunyuan, Relief Institute Shen Kejun and other districts Zhang Yiyi, and civilian representatives such as Wang Yinchong to come to the provincial capital to petition. Central Committee member Shao Lizizhou arrived in Shanghai by early express train from Beijing yesterday morning, accompanied by 晚點遲. The reporter of the Hua Dong News Agency met with the two gentlemen at the station to discuss various matters. The details are recorded as follows:

When the situation in Jinzhou was urgent some time ago, our country telegraphed Minister Shi Zhaoji asking the League of Nations to take appropriate measures to stop the Japanese from advancing into Jinzhou. The station telegraphed Beijing and the Shanghai Transportation Office for instructions. They then received a reply from Beijing instructing them to allow it. The stationmaster informed the representatives of this, and the right to drive the train was taken back by the Railway Bureau. Then the train could drive as usual. Therefore, the dispute over the train was resolved and they were able to drive directly to Shanghai.

Yesterday's Emergency Meeting of All Circles in This City 90

Resolved to Implement People's Self-Defense to Save the Country; Group Representatives to Continue Meeting Today

Youth Association Members, Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, National Progress Association, Postal Workers' Union, Diligent National Products Association, Shanghai Secondary School Youth Association, Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, and other groups convened an emergency meeting yesterday at 3 PM at the Youth Association on Sichuan Road to oppose accepting the humiliating conditions of ceding sovereignty in the Northeast. More than sixty groups participated, with approximately a thousand people in attendance. A resolution was passed to implement the People's Self-Defense to Save the Country. The atmosphere at the meeting was impassioned. The details are recorded below:

Attending Groups: More than sixty groups attended, including the Ten-Person Anti-Japanese National Salvation Group, Taiwan Remnants Association, Money Industry Anti-Japanese Association, Chinese Women's Political Participation Association, China Colonial Border Association, People's Diplomacy Support Association, Japan Research Association, Foreign Firm Chinese Employees Anti-Japanese Association, Party Protection Comrades Association, Pharmaceutical Industry Union, Shanghai Women's Middle School, Southeast Five Provinces Anti-Japanese Association, First District Shipbuilding Association, Cloth Industry Anti-Japanese Workers Union, Zhengfeng College, Ministry of Transportation Telecommunications School, Third District Dyeing Industry Anti-Japanese Association, Mahjong Industry Anti-Japanese Association, Western District Yarn Industry Union, Ai Qun Girls' School, Flying Flower Union, Ham Industry Guild, etc.

Meeting Proceedings: At the beginning of the meeting, Yin Zhiling, Wu Mai, Zhang Shaojie, Wu Ziqian, and Tan Zhibo were publicly elected as the presidium. Miao Zhijie and Liu Xiaozhou served as recorders. After the presidium took their seats, the entire assembly stood in silent tribute for three minutes to mourn the compatriots who died in the Northeast. Then, Yin Zhiling, the chairman, reported on the purpose of the meeting, stating that since the "September 18th Incident," when the Northeast was forcibly occupied by Japan, the Chinese government has relied on the League of Nations, hoping it would resolve the issue. However, after various meetings of the League of Nations, there were no results, and instead, five major conditions were proposed, including establishing Jinzhou as a neutral zone under international management, which the Chinese government has implicitly acquiesced to. If the Chinese government accepts these conditions, it would be tantamount to surrendering the entire Great China to other countries and inviting its own demise. Furthermore, yesterday's newspapers reported that the Dutch Minister Shih K'o-kung suddenly proposed at the League of Nations meeting to place Tianjin under international co-governance. However, today's newspapers reported that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in the capital did not mention this case when hosting the press yesterday at noon. Therefore, the origin of this proposal deserves attention. The purpose of today's meeting is to discuss remedial measures regarding this type of incident. Subsequently, Wu Mai reported, stating that in this critical time of national peril, we should fight the invaders with our blood. Then, Tan Zhibo, Zhang Shaojie, and others delivered speeches that were very impassioned.

Passing Resolutions: After the speeches, more than fifty draft resolutions were discussed. The preparatory committee then presented a general proposal after revisions by the assembly, namely, "Implement People's Self-Defense to Save the Country." A resolution was passed, and each group present elected one official representative to be responsible for organizing a joint national salvation association to discuss and implement the measures. Afterwards, a photograph was taken, and the meeting adjourned. The meeting of the group representatives is scheduled to be held at the Youth Association again at 7 PM tomorrow to discuss and decide on the implementation of the resolutions.

Commemoration of the Zhaohai Warship Uprising Held Yesterday 97

Yesterday was the 16th anniversary of the Zhaohai Warship Uprising. The Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters specially convened representatives from all circles of the city to hold a commemorative meeting. Approximately 300 representatives attended. Chairman Chen Kecheng reported on the facts of the uprising and the significance of the commemoration, and elaborated on the efforts and directions we should take in the future. The details of the meeting are recorded below:

Meeting Order: (1) Entire body stand at attention; (2) Sing the Party song; (3) Pay the highest respect to the Party and National flag and the portrait of the Premier; (4) Chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will; (5) Silence; (6) Chairman's report; (7) Speeches; (8) Slogans; (9) Adjournment.

Attending Representatives: Yang Zheng, Hang Ding'an (Social Affairs Bureau); Xu Jingzhi (Cotton Textile Workers' Union); Yang Youren (Publishing Workers' Union); Yu Hongzhang, Lu Dafu (Civil Shipping Workers' Union); Wang Bingkui (Wine Making Workers' Union); Yu Guoying, Pan Shangsun (Dyeing Workers' Union); Qin Hegao (Quanzhang Middle School); Hu Jinglin (Cigarette Workers' Union); Yao Suikai (Coal and Firewood Workers' Union); and representatives from all levels of Party headquarters, all agencies, and all groups, totaling more than 300 people.

Chairman's Report: Sixteen years ago, on December 5th, 1915, the Party's martyr Mr. Chen Yingzhi, acting on the Premier's orders, gathered comrades in Shanghai to orchestrate the great mission of the Zhaohai Warship Uprising, with the aim of capturing Shanghai as the vanguard for the national campaign against Yuan Shikai. At that time, Mr. Chen Yingzhi was in charge, Mr. Chiang Kai-shek was the planner, and Mr. Yang Hu was the executor. Mr. Chiang's plan was to occupy the warship and fort while actively attacking the arsenal. As a result of the revolutionary comrades' efforts, the Zhaohai warship was safely occupied, but the land attack failed due to strict defenses. Although the matter did not succeed, it was as great and heroic as the March 29th Guangzhou Uprising, and it was even more important for intensifying the Yunnan Uprising and overthrowing Yuan Shikai. Yuan Shikai seized the presidency of the Republic of China through the Xinhai Revolution but did not think of being loyal to the Republic, instead acting perversely, not only betraying his oath but also revealing his ambition for an imperial system, even colluding with Japan as foreign aid, allowing Japanese imperialism to take advantage of the European war to occupy Qingdao. Yuan Shikai did not hesitate to betray the country, agreeing to the Twenty-One Demands as an exchange condition for recognizing the imperial system, becoming so insane that the Party's Premier Sun Yat-sen, seeing this crisis, assigned responsibilities to actively carry out the campaign against Yuan. The Zhaohai Uprising was one of its initiatives. Although the grand and heroic Zhaohai Uprising did not succeed, it terrified Yuan Shikai, and anti-Yuan armies rose up everywhere. Yuan Shikai felt increasingly threatened and died in distress and anger. The foundation of the Republic was saved from danger. This is not only the glorious history of the Party but also the key to the revival of the Republic of China. Sixteen years have passed since then. The foundation of the country is even more shaky than before, and the invasion of foreign powers is even worse than before. Looking at the past and thinking about the present, mixed feelings arise. The Zhaohai Uprising was a matter of sixteen years ago. The courage of the comrades at that time to sacrifice themselves for the country was unmatched in the world. It is almost impossible to find such people today. Even cooperating and working together is hesitant and awkward, which is why the national crisis is lighter in the past and heavier today. It is even more unsurprising that solving the national crisis is easier in the past and more difficult today. If we have the same heroic and fearless determination as we did then, what difficulty would there be in resisting Japanese imperialism? What difficulty would there be in suppressing the domestic Red bandits? If we continue to focus on personal prejudices and desires for power, then the national crisis in the future will be unpredictable, and the nation's peril will be unimaginable. This is what our comrades should deeply reflect on, awaken to, and unite to urgently. The Japanese imperialists' ambition to invade our country has been around for a long time. In 1915, they had already revealed their sharp edge. If there were no righteous people of Zhaohai who fought bravely and killed the enemy, China would not know what it would be like today. Up to now, the Party's military strength has spread throughout the country, but the political foundation has not yet been stabilized, causing foreign insults to come and bandits to run rampant. In the future, how should the whole country unite sincerely to plan for internal stability and external resistance in order to save our dying country? Otherwise, we will have no way to face the righteous people of Zhaohai, no way to face the national masses, and even have no way to see the Premier underground in the future. I hope that we will all act together and strive for it.

Meeting Slogans: (1) Commemorate the great Zhaohai Uprising; (2) The Zhaohai Uprising is the key to the revival of the Republic of China; (3) The Zhaohai Uprising is to overthrow Yuan Shikai; (4) The Zhaohai Uprising is to resist the invasion of the Japanese barbarians; (5) Continue the spirit of the Zhaohai Uprising; (6) Compatriots across the country, unite; (7) Achieve peaceful reunification; (8) Forever break off economic relations with Japan; (9) Strive for military training; (10) Recover the lost territories of the Northeast; (11) Down with Japanese imperialism; (13) Long live the Chinese Kuomintang; (14) Long live the Republic of China.

Second Batch of Premier Stamps Arrives in Shanghai 98

To Be Distributed to All Postal Districts Nationwide Within Days

Martyr Stamps to Arrive in Shanghai by Year-End, Issued on New Year's Day

The Premier Commemorative Stamps were previously ordered by the Post Administration Bureau to be issued on November 12th in all postal districts nationwide. However, since a portion of the first batch of stamps arriving in Shanghai still needed to undergo reproduction procedures before they could be issued, and the supply office in Shanghai had limited inventory, only Beijing and Shanghai first issued and used them on the due date. Other provincial postal districts had to wait until the new stamps being shipped were delivered to Shanghai before the supply office could gradually send them to various districts. It is learned that the second batch of two-fen and four-fen Premier stamps sent by the De La Rue printing company in England arrived at sea yesterday, totaling fifty large boxes, with a total number of approximately 100 to 150 million. Because the postal authorities are routinely closed on Saturdays and Sundays, starting tomorrow (Monday), after the supply office distributes a fixed number, it will gradually send them to the 23 domestic postal districts based on the distance of the postal routes. It is reported that each district can be delivered for sale within this year. The third batch of new manual stamps will arrive in Shanghai by the end of the year. The martyr's portrait stamps printed by the Beiping Ministry of Finance Printing Bureau are being rushed. The General Bureau has now decided that if the stamps are delivered within the year, they will be issued on New Year's Day in 1932.

National Products Alliance Held Regular Meeting Yesterday 100

The National Products Promotion Grand Alliance Committee held its eighth regular meeting of the third session at the association hall on Nine-Mu Land yesterday at 3 PM. Chairman Ji Jiannan presided over the meeting, performed the customary rituals, and reported on the meeting. Discussions and resolutions: (1) Emergency motion to oppose direct Sino-Japanese negotiations: It was resolved to send a telegram requesting the Central National Government, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and Commanders Jiang and Zhang to comply with public opinion and resolutely reject direct Sino-Japanese negotiations. (2) Review of the organizational outline: It was resolved to amend and pass it article by article through a third reading. (3) Review of the budget for expenses: It was resolved to pass the original proposal. (4) Election of standing committee members and committee members of various sections: It was resolved that each group would separately nominate and report to the association. (5) Introduction of disaster victims to factory work: It was resolved to send a letter to each group to notify the factories. (6) Assistance with the raw material dispute between the Yuanchang and Yiheng factories: It was resolved to publicly nominate Chen Yiting, Shi Jie'an, and Ji Jiannan as three committee members responsible for investigating and handling the matter. (7) Certification of the production of the Dachunghua matches: It was resolved to prepare a letter of certification. (8) Juhao requests assistance with the raw material dispute: It was resolved that the firm does not have membership in any group factory or association, so it is not convenient to accept the request. (9) Zhejiang Deqing Farmers' Association requests the design of mechanized homespun cloth: It was resolved to publicly nominate Committee Member Shen Shuyu to review. (10) Ningbo Compatriots Association and eight elementary schools request an investigation of Japanese waxed paper: It was resolved that it is not within the scope of national products, so it is not convenient to investigate. (11) Wang Yan requests maintenance for publishing national products publications: It was resolved to hand it over to the propaganda section for design and handling. There were also six other proposals, and it was decided to postpone the discussion to the next meeting because the statutory time had been extended by 30 minutes.

Wang Jingwei and Others Yesterday Hosted a Banquet for Guangdong's Withdrawing Representatives 101

Mr. Wang Gave a Very Long Speech

Wang Jingwei and Guangdong's representatives hosted a banquet for all withdrawing representatives, numbering over 200 people, yesterday at noon at the Dongya Restaurant in the name of the presidium of the Guangdong withdrawing representatives. All seven members of the presidium, Wang Jingwei, Chen Bijun, Gu Mengyu, Wang Faqin, Guo Chuntao, Zhao Pilian, and Bai Yunti, personally received the guests. The hosts and guests conversed freely until 2:30 PM. During the banquet, Mr. Wang Jingwei, on behalf of the entire presidium, gave a very long speech, encouraging the representatives on how to struggle in the future. The speech is recorded below:

Mr. Wang Jingwei's Speech: "Fellow comrades, today we invite you to this gathering. The preparations were extremely simple and not very respectful. However, before we leave Jing, we have the opportunity to meet here, which is a very valuable opportunity. Today, the presidium has entrusted me to say a few words. What I will be talking about today is primarily about our future joint work. As for the election issue and the Central Committee member issue, these are very small matters. The term of office for the Central Committee members is only one or two years. We should focus entirely on our methods of joint work and joint struggle, especially in this time of crisis for the Party and the nation, and particularly with Japan's dispatch of troops to the Northeast and the tense diplomatic situation. I would like to first report to everyone on the process of this election. When the peace conference in Shanghai had just ended, the seven of us, along with the six representatives from Guangdong and Mr. Hu Zhantang, sent a telegram to the Guangdong Extraordinary Conference proposing to adopt the limited joint election method for the upcoming Fourth Plenary Session election of 24 Central Committee members, with each vote electing eight people, because this method of election would allow both the majority and minority to have the opportunity to be elected. The Guangdong side immediately telegraphed back their approval. Therefore, the number of our withdrawing representatives in Shanghai, over 200, is more than one-third of the total of over 500 representatives. Therefore, we elected ten Central Committee members in Shanghai. This meaning was already stated at the previous meeting. A few days ago, we received two telegrams from Guangzhou. One was from Comrade Sun Zhesheng, saying that the Fourth Plenary Session in Guangzhou had overturned the limited election method, and his words expressed infinite indignation. The second telegram was from Comrade Li Zongren, saying that the Fourth Plenary Session decided that the presidium would introduce 14 candidates for Central Committee members, and the representative assembly would introduce 24 candidates for the election, and then the general assembly would hold a re-election. After receiving these two telegrams, we believe that the Fourth Plenary Session in Guangzhou cannot do this, because in fact, we came to Guangzhou entirely for cooperation. The number of representatives leaving Guangzhou this time is also more than one-third, so the election on December 3rd was very fair. Today, according to the reports, the Guangzhou side has elected 24 Central Committee members, and our list has not been accepted by them. This was expected. However, no matter what, I, representing the presidium and my fellow comrades, can responsibly say that we will definitely do our best to maintain the results of the election of representatives in Shanghai. We may use moderate means to fight for it, or even not be Central Committee members, as long as we achieve our goal. The second point is about our future joint work. This is what we should pay the most attention to. What we need most now is our joint action. The action of a revolutionary party member should be governed by reason. If one can govern their actions with reason, then power cannot subdue them, and wealth cannot move them. But how can we have joint action? Because there is a common proposition. To have a common proposition, we must first have a common discussion. But discussion is not an easy thing, so we must first have a common research. But research alone is not enough. It is easy for an individual to govern their thoughts with reason, but it is difficult to govern their actions with reason. For example, social malpractices often have the knowledge that they are contemptible in reason, but their actions are infected by them. So we must first talk about the issue of integrity. We must have integrity and then have a revolutionary personality. Therefore, we must first jointly encourage integrity to cultivate revolutionary figures. Only with a revolutionary personality can we achieve revolutionary achievements. In this way, we must first jointly encourage integrity, then have joint research, have joint research, then have joint discussion, have joint discussion, then have joint proposition, and have joint proposition, then have joint action. This is our common need. So how should we work together? From now on, we should follow this method to seek joint efforts. In the future, if we are scattered, we should have very close communication methods. If we gather together, we should have opportunities for discussion at all times. We are together in common, and we are also in common when we are not together. We jointly encourage integrity, jointly research, jointly discuss, jointly propose, and jointly act. From the individual to the Party to the nation, we are all fighting together in this way. As for the day of death, it also begins here. Therefore, our unity is a union of reason and is by no means for the small matter of Central Committee members. Everything we do is guided by reason to achieve the goal of joint action. Only in this way can we have a revolutionary personality, and only with a revolutionary personality can we shoulder the revolutionary cause. Conversely, if we do not take reason as our guide, do not encourage integrity, then we cannot have joint research, cannot have joint discussion, cannot have joint proposition, and cannot have joint action. So, at today's banquet, I am putting forward this idea for self-encouragement and to encourage all comrades. I wish all comrades good health."

County Winter Grain Tax Officially Begins Collection Yesterday 103

Tax Rate of Seven Mace, Eight Candareens, Four Cash Per Mu

The Shanghai County Finance Bureau yesterday issued a public notice on the commencement of the winter grain tax, stating that, according to the county's collection of the 20th year winter grain tax, the collection period is set from the 5th day of the 12th month of the national calendar to the 4th day of the 2nd month of the 21st year. Upon investigation, the upper paddy fields and ponds of the 16th, 18th, and 21st Bao of Shangxiang shall be levied nine sheng of rice per mu (calculated at eleven mu, one fen, one li, one hao to equal one shi of complete rice). The permitted embankment paddy fields and ponds shall be levied nine sheng and five ge of rice per mu (calculated at ten mu, five fen, two li, seven hao to equal one shi of complete rice). Each shi is converted into five yuan of silver for regular and supplementary taxes and three jiao of silver for collection fees. In addition, two yuan per shi is levied for grain conversion. This year, the provincial order extends the limit by one year, stamping the serial number and collecting the protection donation of four fen per mu (four jiao, four fen, four li, four hao per shi), and the road construction donation of five fen per mu (five jiao, five fen, five li, six hao per shi). The total tax should be eight yuan and three jiao per shi (seven jiao, four fen, seven li per mu). Furthermore, the upper paddy fields and ponds of the 24th and 26th Bao of Shangxiang, as well as the permitted embankment paddy fields and ponds, shall be levied nine sheng and five ge of rice per mu (calculated at ten mu, five fen, two li, seven hao to equal one shi of complete rice). Each shi is converted into five yuan of silver for regular and supplementary taxes and three jiao of silver for collection fees. In addition, according to the provincial order, two yuan per shi is levied for grain conversion, and the protection donation of four fen per mu (four jiao, two fen, one li, one hao per shi), and the road construction donation of five fen per mu (five jiao, two fen, six li, four hao per shi) are also collected. The total tax should be eight yuan, two jiao, four fen, eight li per shi (seven jiao, eight fen, four li per mu). The deadline is the 4th day of the 2nd month of the 21st year. Those who fail to pay within the two-month limit will be charged a late payment fee of one-tenth. In addition to issuing easily understood notices separately to urge payment and reporting it, the date of commencement of the 20th year winter grain tax, as well as the converted silver yuan for the winter grain tax and the various types of additional levies, are hereby announced to all grain households in the county so that you are all aware of it. You must pay the 20th year grain tax and various levies under your name in full at the counter within the prescribed time limit. Do not delay, lest you incur punishment. This is urgent.

Anti-Japanese Meeting Resolution of Workers at Japanese Merchants' Wharves 104

The Shanghai Municipal Japanese Merchants' Wharf Workers Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association held its first standing committee meeting yesterday. Chairman Liu Xingbo performed the formalities. The following resolutions were discussed: (1) Based on the resolution of the previous executive committee, each wharf shall nominate workers to be responsible for registration matters and submit a list for public decision. Resolution: The list shall be sent by letter to those appointed to take full responsibility, and it shall be adopted. (2) The Shanghai Wharf Workers' Association forwarded a letter from the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Associations of various circles stating that a traitorous merchant at Huangpu Wharf was transporting and selling Japanese coal. The matter was handed over to the investigation division for strict investigation before replying by letter. (3) The investigation division proposed that the workers at each wharf are currently experiencing extreme panic due to the increasing pressure of livelihood and requested immediate relief. Resolution: The propaganda division will convene all workers to promote propaganda as much as possible based on the previous case. (4) The association should hire two secretaries and employ them through examinations. The meeting adjourned.

Now that the diplomacy is urgent and the work is becoming more and more important, it seems that it is not something that I, like Xiaolai, can do all day long. I hereby resign to give way to the virtuous and capable. As for Xiaolai's position as chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, the salvation of the country and the protection of merchants are equally important. I hereby send this letter to request that you follow the example and grant it. I am very grateful to the Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association."

Local News Two

Unscrupulous Nephew Slashes and Kills Uncle, Aunt, and Cousin 110

Three Out of Four Family Members Die

Nephew Is Vicious and Repays Kindness with Enmity

Perpetrator Escapes with Over a Hundred Yuan

Wang Zhenyuan Survives on the Third Floor

Yesterday morning, a bloody case occurred at the Wang Yuanxing Lumber Shop at the intersection of Dongxi Huade Road and Gongping Road. The deceased were the shop owner Wang Jiashun, his wife Jiang, and their eldest son, Xingbao. All three had their heads slashed open and fingers chopped off, a gruesome sight. The perpetrator, Wang's nephew Wang Songfa, fled without a trace after committing the crime. The details are as follows:

Operating Lumber Shop for Nearly Ten Years: Wang Jiashun, a 54-year-old Ningbo native, has been operating the Wang Yuanxing Lumber Shop at 1673 Dongxi Huade Road for nearly ten years. The business is doing well, with annual profits. Wang usually lives frugally and has some savings. His wife, Jiang, is 44 years old and has a son and a daughter. The eldest son, Xingbao, is 16 years old and studies at Chengzhong School. The younger daughter, Zhenyuan, is 16 years old and sews at home. The shop employs three old clerks and three apprentices.

A Nephew Who Is Extremely Unscrupulous: Wang has a nephew named Songfa, 24 years old. His father, Jinmu, works at the Li Yun Yarn Factory in Jiangyin. Songfa has been unscrupulous since childhood and used to be a coppersmith. He is currently unemployed. His father hates him to the bone, so he stays in Shanghai and eats at his uncle's shop. Wang takes pity on his poverty and generously takes him in. Who knew that taking in a vicious person would cause harm and he would be murdered. It is truly tragic.

Songfa Suddenly Returns to the Shop to Ask for Clothes: The night before last, Wang went out to bathe. After the shop assistants finished closing up, they spent time playing cards for entertainment. Wang's wife, Jiang, was chatting upstairs with relatives and children when Songfa suddenly arrived at the shop. He first watched them play cards in the shop hall. Around 11 o'clock, Wang returned from his bath and went upstairs into the room. Songfa followed him up and said to his uncle, "The weather is getting colder, and I lack clothes. Please make me a cotton coat." Wang agreed. Songfa went downstairs to sleep. It was already late, and Wang and his wife undressed and went to bed together. His son, Xingbao, slept in another bed.

Three People Killed with a Hatchet: Around 2 o'clock in the morning, Songfa suddenly got up, took a hatchet used by the old clerks in the shop, went straight upstairs, pried open the door, and saw Wang and Jiang fast asleep. He immediately stepped forward and swung the hatchet, first striking Wang's head with a heavy blow, splitting it open. At the same time, he also struck Jiang with a blow, and blood flowed all over the bed. Jiang died on the spot, while Wang was still sitting up and resisting with his hands. Songfa immediately raised the hatchet and slashed wildly, severing all his fingers. At this time, Xingbao also woke up and shouted. Fearing that the matter would be revealed, Songfa turned around and struck Xingbao's head, killing him instantly. Seeing that all three were dead, Songfa pried open the silver box in the room and took over a hundred silver yuan. He also seized over fifty yuan from Wang's side and hurriedly went downstairs and escaped through the back door.

Tragic Case Only Discovered in the Morning: When the bloody case occurred, the shop assistants sleeping downstairs heard the noise but thought it was a quarrel between husband and wife and did not pay attention. They did not know anything when they opened the door in the morning. Later, Zhenyuan got up and entered the room and saw her parents dead on the bed and her brother dead on the ground. She was shocked and cried loudly. The shop assistants downstairs went upstairs to see and knew that a great disaster had occurred. They immediately reported it to the Huishan Police Station, which ordered Chinese and foreign detectives to investigate the scene. The shop assistants were all arrested and questioned. In the afternoon, the three corpses were taken to the forensic examination office on Feilun Road. The examination will be held the day after tomorrow on Sunday. A plaid duck-tongue cap that Wang Songfa usually wore was found at the time.

Wang Zhenyuan Fortunately Escapes: Of the four members of Wang Jiashun's family, three died tragically, which is heartbreaking to hear. Wang's daughter Zhenyuan was originally sleeping in the same room as her parents, but it happened that her father's niece-in-law had come to Shanghai that day and was temporarily sleeping on the third floor, otherwise she would have been harmed as well. It was a misfortune within a misfortune.

Father and Daughter-in-Law Commit Adultery, Violent Father Gouges Out Son's Eyes 111

The World's Customs Are Declining, and Ethics Are Greatly Changed

Yang Tingchen Is Truly Old and Shameless

Actually Regards His Son as a Thorn in His Side

The Court Should Impose Severe Punishment

Yesterday, in the grass shed at No. 14 Xinqiao Road, in the jurisdiction of the Second District General Office in Nanshi, an incident occurred in which a father and daughter-in-law committed adultery, and the violent father suddenly became angry and tied his son to a wooden stake with an iron chain and gouged out his eyes with a sharp knife, a tragic scene unprecedented in the world. Fortunately, the chief of the Liyuan Road Police Station noticed it and rescued his son. The violent father and his accomplice were arrested on the spot. The details are as follows:

Rearing Pigs to Make a Living: Yang Tingchen, from Funing, Jiangbei, is 52 years old. He came to Shanghai a few years ago and used to work as a rickshaw puller. Recently, due to his old age, he has been living in a grass shed at No. 34 Xinqiao Road, Nanshi, rearing piglets to make a living. Yang lost his wife at the age of 38 and only had one son, Yang Xiaotaozi, who is now 29 years old. He is a rickshaw puller and lives in a small boat in the Hebang of Xuxie Road. His wife, Gu, is now 31 years old. The father takes the place of the son. Gu came to Yang's family as a child bride at the age of seven. Xiaotaozi lost his mother at the age of fifteen and married Gu at the age of sixteen. However, his father Tingchen was able to take advantage of his son's youth and deceive him, and he had been a widower for many years, so he was sexually aroused and had an affair with Gu in secret, and he had tasted the flavor of a virgin before his son. Therefore, although the two young people were married in name, Tingchen actually took care of everything. Although Xiaotaozi knew that his father's actions were inappropriate, he was concerned about Gu's reputation once he spoke out, so he always tolerated it and did not speak out.

Accused of Insubordination: Although Yang Xiaotaozi repeatedly tolerated it, his father still wanted to take things further and regarded his son as a thorn in his side. He felt that he could not be happy until he removed him. Therefore, he did not hesitate to nitpick and find fault with everything. In June of this year, the father and son suddenly had a quarrel, and Tingchen actually filed a lawsuit against his son in the local court, accusing him of insubordination. However, the court at that time observed the ancient训 of there is no wrong parent in the world and sentenced Xiaotaozi to two months in prison.

Conspiring and Plotting: Two months passed in the blink of an eye, and Xiaotaozi was released from prison in August. Xiaotaozi then moved his wife Gu out to live separately in order to avoid his father's edge. Unexpectedly, after living peacefully for more than fifty days, Tingchen tried every means to lure Gu out and hide her without a trace. Although Xiaotaozi knew that his father had done it, he did not dare to question him. He could only feel depressed and searched everywhere when he was not pulling his rickshaw. Tingchen was afraid that it would eventually be revealed after a long time and that the trouble in his heart would be unavoidable. Therefore, evil thoughts suddenly arose, and he discussed a plan with his nephew-in-law Zhang Maohuzi (i.e., Zhang Jinkui) and decided to carry it out.

Lured to the Grass Shed: At about 5:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, Zhang Jinkui went to Xuxie Road to meet Xiaotaozi and falsely claimed that his father Tingchen had been searching for his missing daughter-in-law for days without success. He was very anxious and now wanted to go to Tingchen's place to discuss a proper plan and search together to achieve quick results. Xiaotaozi then followed Zhang there. Unexpectedly, as soon as he entered the grass shed, Tingchen's anger was evident, and he saw Yang Bingxing (a 61-year-old beggar) of the same clan sitting there. The father and son had not said a word when Tingchen ordered Zhang Jinkui to help tie Xiaotaozi tightly to a wooden stake that had been planted in advance with an iron chain.

Actually Commits a Heinous Crime: After Tingchen and Jinkui had tied up Xiaotaozi, the two of them sat opposite each other and drank heavily to enhance their mood. It was not until 11:00 p.m., when it was late at night and quiet, that Xiaotaozi saw that the situation was not good and was about to shout for help. However, as soon as he opened his mouth, Tingchen threw lime into his throat, causing Xiaotaozi to be unable to speak. Then, Tingchen used a sharp knife for trimming water chestnuts to gouge out Xiaotaozi's eyes and embedded lime in the eye sockets. Xiaotaozi's pain pierced his heart, and he had no way to call for help and could only leave it to fate.

Patrol Officer Investigates: After Xiaotaozi's eyes were gouged out, Tingchen threatened him, saying that he had to falsely accuse someone of murder, otherwise he would be put to death. Unexpectedly, while he was gloating, Patrol Officer Wang Shengshan of the Liyuan Road Police Station of the Second District General Office, along with Chief Police Shen Chuanxian, were patrolling and heard extremely painful cries from shed No. 14. They went inside to inspect and saw a man tied to a wooden stake with his eyes gouged out and covered in blood. They were shocked and immediately arrested Tingchen and his party and took them all to the Second District General Office.

Escorted to the Court: When Chief Ling of the district heard that such a shocking case of unnatural injury had occurred in his jurisdiction, he immediately conducted a preliminary hearing. First, Xiaotaozi tearfully recounted his experience. Then, according to Tingchen's confession, his son had said that he would harm him with an axe (Tingchen referred to himself) as soon as he was released in August. On the 24th of this month, because his eldest grandson had a stomachache and was crying, his son and daughter-in-law had a quarrel, and his daughter-in-law had fled without a trace. Today, he brought his rebellious son home, and in a moment of anger, he gouged out his eyes. After Chief Ling finished the interrogation, he considered that the case was serious and immediately prepared a document to send it to the court for punishment according to the law.

Record of Yesterday's Trial of the Baoshan Road Tragedy 112

Details of the Injured Person's Experience, Family of the Deceased Petition to Withdraw the Case

The trial of the Baoshan Road tragedy in Zhabei continued yesterday morning in the first courtroom by the criminal court of the local court. The injured person's side retained lawyers Zhang Chongding, Hu Yuanjun, Hu Yuanteng, etc. as litigation agents. The defendant You Boli was still represented by lawyers Sha Xunyi, Zhu Shaowen, and Zhang Yaozeng (Zhang did not arrive and was represented by Qu Yuefu). As for the five patrol officers, the court appointed lawyer Tao Jiachun to provide free defense. The courtroom was already full of spectators at 9:00 a.m., so Police Chief Xu Jinqing and Police Officers Chen Xihui and Chen Junfang were ordered to supervise the police in maintaining order in the courtroom and courtyard. At about 10:00 a.m., after the injured person reported, Criminal Court President Qian Chengjun, along with Judge Zhao Yongzhou, Wu Zhen, Prosecutor Yang Wenjun, and Clerk Yu Bi, arrived at the court. First, the injured person Wang Jiaxiang was questioned. Wang Xiangshou, 21 years old, from Zhenjiang, a coppersmith living at 60 Hexingji Copper Shop, Zhonghua Xin Road, at the intersection of Xibaoxing Road, was asked, "What time were you at the entrance of the Fifth District that day?" He replied, "October 1st." "What time?" "Seven or eight o'clock." "Who did you go with?" "I went with three of my senior brothers." "What are their names?" "Shen Er and Changsheng." "What did you go to do?" "I went to Wuma Road to buy clothes." "Since you went to Wuma Road to buy clothes, how did you get to the entrance of the Fifth District? Did you buy the clothes?" "I went there and came back." "What time did you get to the entrance of the Fifth District?" "Seven or eight o'clock." "What did you do in the Fifth District?" "I don't know." "What time did you leave?" "After I was injured, I was sent to the hospital." "What time were you shot?" "Seven thirty." "Where were you shot?" "In the back." "Was it shot in the left and right shoulders?" "Yes." "Where in the Fifth District were you injured?" "Across from the cigarette and paper shop." "After you were shot, did Shen Er and Changsheng see you?" "They saw me." "What happened after you were shot?" "I ran for fifty or sixty steps and felt pain, and then I fell to the ground. Shen Er and Changsheng hired a rickshaw to send me to the hospital." "Which hospital did you send me to?" "Jisheng Hospital." "Where is Jisheng Hospital?" "Across from the Commercial Press." "What road is it?" "Baoshan Road." "After arriving at the hospital, was the bullet taken out?" "It was taken out." "Where was it taken out?" "In the neck." "After it was taken out, did you see what the bullet looked like?" "It was round." "Where did the bullet come from when you were walking at the entrance?" "I don't know." "Did you see how many people were at the entrance of the Fifth District?" "Seven or eight hundred people." "What were they doing?" "I don't know." "Did you hear what they said in their mouths?" "I'm deaf, I don't know." "When you were investigating, how did you say you were beaten down in the Fifth District?" "I didn't say that." "I've been asking you for a long time. Even if you're not deaf, it doesn't matter if you said a slogan." "I don't know." "Are you willing to file a lawsuit after you were injured?" "I want to file a lawsuit." "Who fired the gun?" "I don't know." "Did you hear many gunshots?" "I heard them." At this point, the official asked the injured person

Shen Xikun, 24 years old, from Changzhou, a coppersmith living at 22 Tianjili, Xianshan Road, was asked, "Do you know Wang Xiangshou?" "I don't know him." "Where were you injured?" "In the buttocks." "How many injuries?" "One injury." "What time were you shot?" "Nine o'clock." "Where were you shot?" "Across from the Fifth District." "What day were you at the Fifth District?" "October 1st." "Why did you go to the Fifth District?" "I wanted to go home and was passing by." "Were you alone or with someone?" "I was alone going to my own home." "Which side of the Fifth District were you shot?" "Across from the Fifth District, at the corner of the market." "Did the gun come from the Fifth District or from the road?" "It came from the Fifth District." "Were there people in front of you?" "I saw a lot of people, so I walked across the street." "What happened after you were injured?" "I entered a clothing store." "What is the name of the store?" "I was dizzy at the time, I don't know." "How did you know you went to the hospital?" "The people in the clothing store sent me to the hospital." "Which hospital did you go to?" "I first went to Jisheng Hospital, but I couldn't get the bullet out, so I went to Tongren Hospital." "Did they take it out?" "They took it out." "Where is Tongren Hospital?" "Across from Peng Road, near the triangular vegetable market." "Did you see the bullet after it was taken out?" "I saw it." "What did it look like?" "It was long, like a finger, about half as long." "When the tailor sent you there, he should have known the name." "I didn't know, and I couldn't speak when I got to Tongren Hospital." "Where did the bullet come from?" "It came from inside the Fifth District." "Who fired it?" "The police." "Do you have a store next to the Fifth District?" "I don't have one." "Why did you say before that the store was next to the Fifth District, and you were shot when you came out of Tianjili? Why is that not right now?" "How many people did you see in the Fifth District?" "More than three thousand people." "Why were they there?" "I don't know." "What did you hear the thousands of people saying?" "They were saying that the district chief dragged the person who posted the slogans in." "Is there anything else?" "Everyone was talking about what was going on in the district, and they wanted to drag the person who posted the slogans in." At this point, the official asked the injured person

Wang Hexing, 25 years old, from Ningbo

Page 16

A coppersmith working at Lian'an Electric Company in Huangpu Wharf, Yangshupu. He lives at 46 Yipinyiwu. The official asked, "Where is Yipinyiwu?" He replied, "Baoshan Road, Qiujiang Road." "What time did you pass by the Fifth District that day?" "October 1st, 7 or 8 p.m." "How many people were walking?" "I was walking alone to find a friend on Xiangshan Road." "Did you walk past the Fifth District?" "There were many people, so I couldn't walk past. I waited a while, and a long-distance bus came. I thought someone had been killed by the bus, so I went to take a look and heard someone shout, 'Fire!'." "Who shouted, 'Fire'?" "The district chief. Later, he also stomped his feet and shouted, 'Fire!' and the bullets came." "Where did they hit you?" "In the foot." "Where were you standing?" "Five or six steps from the entrance of the district." "After I was injured, I saw a rickshaw at the entrance of the alley and called it home." "Did you go to the hospital?" "I went to Jisheng Hospital." "Who sent you there?" "My family sent me there. Later, I also went to Tongren Hospital." "Was the bullet taken out?" "I don't know." "Did you ask the doctor later?" "He said it wasn't taken out. "Each person took 1,300 yuan in cash, and each person also received a savings deposit of 3,500 yuan with a term of ten years." Asked You Boli, "Did you fire the gun that day in the courtyard?" "Yes." "What kind of gun did you fire?" "A Mauser pistol." "How did you fire it?" "I ordered it to be fired into the sky to scare them." "Where did the two people die?" "One with a back injury died far to the east, and one died in front of the district. Yangsi Township Bandits Kill Two 113

Victims Cut Off Bandits' Retreat

Leading to Dozens of Gunshots

Robbery Also Occurs at Wangjia Bridge

Authorities Are Now Strictly Pursuing the Robbers

In Pudong's Yangsi Township (Shangyi Ninth District), farmer Lu Miaogen's house, number seven in Lujia Residence, was suddenly invaded by a large gang of over twenty bandits at approximately one o'clock last night. Each held handguns, knives, and clubs, lying in ambush around the Lu residence. Several of the bandits were wearing blue cloth short shirts and trousers, speaking in a Jiangbei accent. They crashed into the house, and the Lu family, men, women, old, and young, were startled awake from their sleep, immediately driven into a corner and silenced in fear. The bandits then rummaged through boxes and chests, looting approximately sixty yuan in cash, paper money, and foreign currency, several land deeds, and four gold earrings. Dissatisfied with the small amount of loot, they simultaneously broke into the nearby Yang Zhaogui's house at number twelve, searching and looting. Yang seized the opportunity to escape through a side door, joining Miaogen, his son Fujin, and his cousin Abaobao, totaling four people, and ran to the stone bridge embankment behind the residence to wait (this was the bandits' only way back), intending to arrest them. Unexpectedly, the bandits guarding the bridge had already noticed them and violently slashed Miaogen's forehead with a knife, causing brain matter and blood to gush out like a spring. Another bandit immediately fired a gun, with continuous cracking and banging sounds, totaling forty to fifty shots. Miaogen was struck by six or seven bullets in his waist and immediately fell to the ground, dead. Yang Zhaogui suffered two gunshot wounds each to his left wrist and waist. Lu's cousin, Abaobao, had his foot pierced by a bullet. Lu's son, Fujin, was shot in two places on his left thigh and the back of his foot, both collapsing and unable to move. Seeing that they had injured and killed the victims, the bandits fled south and escaped. At dawn, the Lu family carried the injured to Shanghai Hospital for treatment. However, Yang Zhaogui's injuries were fatal, and he had already died upon arrival at the hospital and was carried back home. Abaobao and Fujin's injuries were light and not life-threatening. At nine o'clock yesterday morning, Officer Li, from the Yangsi Bridge Third District Third Precinct police station, reported the incident. The station then relayed the information to the Public Security Bureau, using the telephone to inform all district stations and teams to strictly pursue the stolen goods and bandits. The deceased, Lu Miaogen, was fifty-five years old, and Yang Zhaogui was thirty-six years old, both local residents. Their bodies had not yet been collected by evening. It was also heard that robbery cases occurred at Wangjia Bridge, where the border between the Second District of Shangyi and Nanyi is located, and near Zhuangjia Temple (Nanyi) on the same night. The victims' names have not yet been identified. Yesterday at dawn, the Beicai Town Security Corps intercepted three bandits and a package of stolen clothes, waiting for the victims to identify them.

Fierce Kidnappers Still Attempt to Flee After Being Shot 114

Public Security Bureau Officer Captures Zhejiang Secret Agent Who Came to Shanghai to Arrest Bandits

Not Following Police Station Procedures

Ordered to Pay Bail and Be Available for Summons

Recently, Zhejiang Provincial Government Security Department secret agent Liu Ruibiao learned that Guo Abiao, a wanted kidnapping kingpin from Shaoxing, Zhejiang Province, had repeatedly committed kidnapping and extortion, resisted arrest, and injured people in Zhejiang. He had fled to the Shanghai Concession and gathered followers, planning to strike again. Therefore, he specifically reported to the Security Department Director and prepared official documents, coordinating with the First District Court and the Public Concession Police Department to assist the secret agent in apprehending him upon his arrival in Shanghai. Liu then brought his detective partners, Cui Huisheng, etc., from Hangzhou to Shanghai a few days ago, strictly investigating the bandit leader's whereabouts. The day before yesterday, at dusk, they learned that Guo Abiao was hiding in the Rongsheng Hotel in Puqing Lane, Fujian Road. Liu, without following the usual procedure of first submitting the official documents to the First Special Court and the relevant police station for assistance, immediately assigned his partners Liu Jinbiao, Wang Asi, and Ying Huisan to rush to the Rongsheng Hotel and arrest Guo. The three men reported back to Liu Ruibiao, with one person escorting Guo the bandit elsewhere. Unexpectedly, as soon as they left the Rongsheng Hotel, Guo, relying on his strength, resisted slightly and immediately broke free and fled. Since the captured bandit had escaped, they pursued him relentlessly. They chased one another until the intersection of Fujian Road and Fuzhou Road. The pursuers saw two Chinese constables, numbers 3280 and 3327, standing guard there and shouted for help to catch a thief. The two constables bravely assisted upon hearing the call, but Guo was extremely agile and moved quickly, making it difficult to catch him. The pursuer then took out a handgun and shot at Guo. The two constables also fired one shot each, but all missed. Guo then ran south quickly. At the intersection of Guangdong Road, the two constables fired one shot each again, and Guo was hit by a bullet and collapsed. The pursuers thought he could be captured, but Guo, enduring the pain, jumped up and continued running forward, disappearing in an instant. Fortunately, at that moment, a public security bureau detective, Han, was eating at a dim sum shop at number 275 Guangdong Road and saw a person suddenly rush into a store at number 234 and saw constables chasing him, so he also put down his chopsticks and assisted in the pursuit. When Guo the bandit ran out of the back door of number 234 and fled into Jiu'an Lane, Detective Han happened to be there and intercepted him. The two Chinese constables then arrived. However, the detective partner who was escorting Guo the bandit was nowhere to be found. After a long wait, he did not appear. The two constables then took Guo to the Lao Zha gate police station. The police chief, seeing that Guo was injured, immediately sent Detective Wang Shanxiang to the hospital for treatment. According to Guo's statement to Detective Wang, his name was Ying Dalong, originally from Shaoxing, and Detective Wang temporarily suspended the inquiry about why he was being chased because the doctor urgently needed to treat him. At 9:30 PM, Liu Ruibiao, the secret agent from Hangzhou, having learned that Guo had been captured, brought the official documents and his partner Cui Jinsheng to the Lao Zha gate police station. He stated that the person who had been arrested was the bandit leader Guo Abiao, not Ying Dalong. He also said that after Guo was arrested at the Rongsheng Hotel, he was escorted by Liu Jinbiao, and that Liu Jinbiao had shouted for help and fired the gun when he escaped. The police chief then ordered Detective Wang to go to the hospital again to question the injured person in detail, but he still denied that his name was Guo Abiao and said that the person who chased him and fired the gun was named Wang Asi, not Liu Jinbiao. Detective Wang immediately reported the situation to the police chief for verification. The police chief believed that according to precedent, when mainland government officials arrest criminals in the concession, they should first notify the police station. Since the secret agent did not follow this procedure, his actions could not be considered legal. He detained Liu Ruibiao and Cui Jinsheng. The box cannon, twenty-six bullets, and gun license carried by Liu, as well as the handgun and seventeen bullets carried by Cui, were temporarily confiscated. Yesterday morning, they were all sent to the First Special District Court, where Judge Xu of the Criminal Division conducted a preliminary hearing. The police station lawyer, Ru BaoYi, explained the situation and requested the court to verify whether the injured person denied that his name was Guo Abiao, and if the Zhejiang government officials wanted to identify him as the bandit leader, they should provide evidence to prove it. As for the secret agent's procedural errors, he requested the court to verify them. According to Liu Ruibiao's confession, the person captured was indeed the kidnapping bandit leader Guo Abiao, who had committed numerous crimes in Zhejiang. In addition to kidnapping and extortion, he had also plotted to capture and kill escorts the year before. After the interrogation by Judge Xu, Liu and Cui were released on bail and ordered to be available for summons. At the next court session, Liu Jinbiao and the other three people should be brought to the court, and evidence should be presented to prove that the injured person was indeed Guo Abiao, who had committed crimes, for verification.

Handgun and Uniform Taken With Him

Woman Flees Before Wedding 116

Old Father Hangs Himself

Zhang Yougen, a villager from Zhangjia Residence on the Shanghai-Minhang-Nanzhe Road in the southwest countryside, is nearly forty years old and has only one daughter named Zhao Di, who is eighteen years old. Since she was young, she has been betrothed to Huang Shengyun, a tailor from nearby Zhujia Lane. Although Zhao Di is not beautiful, she likes to dress up. Last year, she asked her father to dissolve the engagement with the Huang family, but Yougen refused, causing Zhao Di to be unhappy. This spring, during the Qingming Festival, Zhao Di used the excuse of going to her relatives' house to sweep the tombs and entered a Buddhist temple as a nun. After repeated questioning by the old nun, she revealed the truth. The nun then notified Yougen to take her back home. The Huang family, learning about this, feared that it would affect the engagement and chose yesterday as the wedding date. However, Zhao Di refused to comply and repeatedly made things difficult for her father. Knowing that she could not change the situation, she ran away alone on the morning of the 2nd of this month while her family was asleep. After his beloved daughter ran away, Yougen asked people to search for her everywhere, but to no avail. The Huang family also gathered many people to demand an explanation. Affected by this, Yougen had the thought of ending his life. The night before last, he hanged himself while people were not paying attention. His wife, Cai, noticed it early and quickly rescued him, giving him ginger soup, and he recovered. Relatives are now mediating between the two families and dissolving the Zhang-Huang engagement. They are also posting notices to find Zhao Di and bring her home to prevent her from wandering elsewhere.

Another Headless Infant Corpse Found 117

Combined With Nameless Head

At 11:45 AM on the 1st of this month, Liu Qingxiang, a minor worker number two from the Public Works Department Health Bureau, discovered the severed head of an infant next to a trash can at number 165 in a lane near Parker Road. Liu reported this to the Xinzha police station, who ordered detectives to investigate. The infant's head was sent to the Philan Road mortuary for examination. The next morning, Prosecutor Guo from the First Special Court arrived at the mortuary for examination and ordered it to be temporarily handed over to the forensic doctor for preservation. As reported previously, Chinese constables number 1065 and 347 of the police station passed by Mahou Road at approximately 4:00 AM on the 29th of last month and saw a Chinese man carrying a box and abandoning it on the east side of the road before fleeing. However, the two constables did not suspect that there was a headless infant corpse inside. The box was later transported back to the Putuo Mountain Villa Mortuary by the Dachang rear police station. The discovery of a head led to a thorough investigation, and they transferred the box back from Dachang to inspect it, confirming that there was a headless infant corpse inside. The corpse was immediately sent to the mortuary. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo from the Special Court arrived at the mortuary for examination. Forensic doctor Wei Ligong and the Public Works Department doctor stated that the head was indeed severed from the corpse and confirmed that it was a Chinese girl. Mr. Guo also questioned the two Chinese constables. He then ordered that the corpse of the unnamed female infant who had died and had been examined should be combined with the previously examined unnamed head and handed over to the Pushan Mountain Villa for burial. The police station is strictly pursuing the murderer and will investigate and punish them.

Large Quantity of Military Supplies Discovered in Cement on Sandboat 118

Shao Weijun, a 54-year-old from Ganyu, opened the Sanxin Company at No. 5 Alley, Muming Lane, Cuifeng Street, Nanshi. Yesterday at about 1:00 PM, Xu Jishi, the captain of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's water patrol team, led detectives Wang Jiheng and other police officers to discover a Mauser pistol, 118 bullets, two opium lamps, and eight opium bubbles under a clothing box on the second floor of the building. Captain Xu strictly questioned the whereabouts of the large quantity of cement brought in. It was reported that it had been transported to the sandboat on the Pubin side opposite the First District Headquarters at Maojia Alley. The two men, along with the seized evidence, were taken to the First District and then back to the team. Then, under the direction of the men, the police officers took a boat to the sandboat indicated by Xian Zuoqing and opened the approximately twenty barrels of cement one by one. After more than an hour, they discovered thirty-one Mauser pistols, two two-inch Lejia guns, two Mauser pistols, one Browning pistol, and 3,020 bullets in four of the barrels. The entire collection was taken back to the team. Captain Xu believed that the case was extremely serious and immediately brought Xian Yin and the two men in for a preliminary hearing. Shao Weijun confessed that the military supplies were actually transported by customers Xian Zuoqing and a Mr. Li, and that he did not know the real situation. Xian Zuoqing, 38 years old, from Juzhou, Shandong, confessed that the military supplies were purchased by his friend Li Xiuchen and five other people and mixed into the cement barrels. They were transported to Juzhou on a sandboat. He only bought one large and one small gun, along with the ones he bought in Yemen, and transported them back to his hometown for self-defense. They had spent a lot of effort coming up with this secret method of smuggling guns, but they never expected to be discovered. They usually smoked opium in the Taixin Hotel in the French Concession. Detectives were immediately dispatched to the Taixin Hotel to arrest those people, but they had already fled. Captain Xu ordered a document to be prepared and had Xian Zuoqing and Shao Weijun, along with the seized military supplies and opium, sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for questioning and punishment.

Record of the General Meeting of the Shanghai Raw Cattle and Sheep Leather Industry 121

The entire Shanghai raw cattle and sheep leather industry was outraged by the harsh implementation of the raw cattle and sheep leather export inspection rules issued by the Commodity Inspection Bureau without the consent of the leather merchants. Therefore, a general meeting was held at the Leather Merchants Association on Beihai Road at 5:00 PM yesterday. More than 40 people attended the meeting. Chairman Zhu, as well as Song Zigang, a representative from the Dangyouli Foreign Firm, and Wu Liangmei, a representative from the Shenyu Foreign Firm, reported that the export of supported buffalo leather that had been agreed upon by both the buyer and seller was repeatedly hindered by the Inspection Bureau, which refused to release it, resulting in missed shipping dates and heavy losses. The attendees were even more indignant upon hearing this report. They all believed that raw cattle and sheep leather was not comparable to silk flowers and did not require inspection. However, out of respect for the government, they made concessions and paid for the inspection. Now, the bureau's inspection methods are so harsh that they affect the leather merchants' capital. It is necessary to demand reform. It was unanimously decided to appoint six fellow merchants, including Mr. Zhu, as representatives to go to the Inspection Bureau to petition at 3:00 PM yesterday (the 5th). If the bureau cannot provide a satisfactory response, they will go to the Ministry of Industry in the capital to petition. At that time, all the facts of the bureau's violation of commercial sentiment will be published in the newspaper.

Reader Communication: Three Notices to All Readers of Reader Correspondence 135

Research on Ma Zhanshan

All readers highly respect General Ma Zhanshan. Some have written letters expressing gratitude and weeping tears of gratitude. Some have pawned clothes and sold property to donate to the military. Some have traveled far together, willing to risk their lives to rescue him. This shows that the people's hearts are not dead and justice is clear. In fact, General Ma Zhanshan is only fulfilling his duty. As the military officer in charge of border defense, he naturally has the responsibility to defend the territory and resist the enemy. General Ma's great admiration by the people is only because he is in an atmosphere of non-resistance. Suddenly, he is even more pleasing and admirable, almost prostrate.

I hope that readers will not just say a few good words about Ma Zhanshan and shed a few drops of hot tears. At least, they must further study the following questions:

(1) In this time of national crisis, why is Ma Zhanshan and his subordinates the only ones who resist the enemy and are not afraid of death?

(2) What kind of education was Ma Zhanshan raised in?

(3) Can the current general education raise Ma Zhanshan?

I heard that Ma Zhanshan has not read many books and knows few words. He came from the ranks and rose step by step to his current position as a low-level and mid-level military officer. Not only is new education completely out of the question, but old education also has little relationship. I think the only education he received was novels, ballads, and dramas, or the stories of loyalty, filial piety, and integrity passed down by the elders in his hometown. He has actually done a great job of defending the country and winning glory. A general who advocates non-resistance, although he did not graduate from a certain university, is still a college student. Is there still a lot to consider about whether the old morality and old culture that today's celebrities despise should be overthrown and kicked over with one punch and one kick?

What we usually believe in is not science saving the country? Thinking of the smashing of theocracy and the abandonment of ethics, is not the rule of law spirit to replace them in the future? The publicity of general celebrities in words and the promotion of tongues ultimately boils down to this. Today, Ma Zhanshan is a lone army in a desperate situation, using a small number of troops and a few remaining weapons to resist Japan's all-out army, and he is surrounded by a vast and unhelpful situation. From a scientific point of view, there is no chance of survival, only surrender to seek survival. Even with the rule of law spirit, there are leaders who advocate non-resistance and precedents of giving up and retreating. Is it illegal to act on orders? Ma Zhanshan's actions are simply not tolerated by scientists' logic and not dreamed of by those who advocate the rule of law, but he is praised by the general public with congratulatory telegrams for "awakening the national soul for China and regaining the national character for the nation." Then, is it only advocating science and the rule of law, if not the problem of right and wrong, I am afraid there is still not enough problem.

I know that there are many Ma Zhanshans in the Northeast Army in addition to Officer Ma Zhanshan, and there are still many Ma Zhanshans in officers everywhere. They are only suppressed by general non-resistance leaders, so there is no opportunity to use their talents and become famous. We ordinary people have no private relationship with Ma Zhanshan and are ready to transport unlimited amounts of hot blood and bitter tears to the emerging hundreds of millions of Ma Zhanshans. The tyrant has no desire. If the good men and good citizens do not take this opportunity to perform meritorious service and serve the country, when will they wait? I ask all the readers of Reader Correspondence, if you all agree with my words? In addition to replying to the letters separately, public announcements will be temporarily suspended for the next few days. Sincerely,

The Xu Jia Hui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the coastal areas of this region and the Yangtze River basin would be mostly cloudy, with morning fog. Winds along the Shandong coast would be variable. Northeast winds would prevail south of Ma'an Island. A hurricane east of Mindanao continued its northwestward movement.
